At the End of a Lover's Quest
//The droning turns to a sudden ringing. Knees, buckled. Face, firm against the soil. Eyes, no longer under control.//\n\nYour wish is granted. Your lover will walk the earth, as you have made genuine sacrifice.\n\n//The earth vibrates against the cheek, telegraphing the futile blows of a mortal's anguish//\n\n[[I'm sorry.|Sorry]]
//The droning becomes ever louder as the archway approaches. A figure appears in the distance. Followed? No...//\n\nYour wish is granted. Your lover will walk the earth under the guise of the image manifested in the deepest regions of your heart.\n\n//Droning.\n\nThe empty eyes. Motionless stance. Unable to speak. Unable to love. The dead may walk, but no soul has ever walked among the living.//\n\n[[//fin//|Start]]

//One confident swing connects. The head of the stranger now severed, the droning weakens. Foreign blood streams down the deity's earthly throne.\n\nFootsteps are head from behind. The once deceased places an outstretched hand over the forehead of the living. The droning is louder than before, though it is without discomfort.//\n\nThank you.
